import os import requests import json from bs4 import BeautifulSoup from urllib.parse import urljoin, quote from datetime import datetime import networkx as nx import matplotlib.pyplot as plt from collections import defaultdict def create_directory_if_not_exists(directory): """Create a directory if it doesn't exist""" if not os.path.exists(directory): os.makedirs(directory) return directory # Create workspace directory workspace_dir = 'workspace' create_directory_if_not_exists(workspace_dir) # Function to get a specific Wikipedia page version on a date def get_wikipedia_specific_version(title, date_str): """Get the version of a Wikipedia page as it existed on the specified date""" print(f"Retrieving Wikipedia page for '{title}' as it appeared on {date_str}...") # Convert date format from YYYY-MM-DD to YYYYMMDD for API date_formatted = date_str.replace('-', '') # Step 1: Use the MediaWiki API to find the revision closest to the target date api_url = f"https://en.wikipedia.org/w/api.php" params = { 'action': 'query', 'prop': 'revisions', 'titles': title, 'rvlimit': 1, 'rvprop': 'ids|timestamp', 'rvstart': f"{date_formatted}000000", # Start of the day in format YYYYMMDDHHMMSS 'format': 'json' } try: print(f"Querying Wikipedia API for revision ID on {date_str}...") headers = {'User-Agent': 'WikipediaNavigationResearch/1.0 (research project)'} response = requests.get(api_url, params=params, headers=headers) response.raise_for_status() # Raise an exception for HTTP errors data = response.json() # Extract revision ID from the API response pages = data.get('query', {}).get('pages', {}) if not pages: print(f"No page data returned for {title}") return None, None page_id = next(iter(pages.keys())) page_data = pages[page_id] if page_id == '-1' or 'missing' in page_data: print(f"Page {title} not found") return None, None revisions = page_data.get('revisions', []) if not revisions: print(f"No revisions found for {title} on or before {date_str}") return None, None revision = revisions[0] revision_id = revision.get('revid') timestamp = revision.get('timestamp') print(f"Found revision {revision_id} from {timestamp}") # Step 2: Construct the URL for the specific revision encoded_title = quote(title) revision_url = f"https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title={encoded_title}&oldid={revision_id}" return revision_url, revision_id except Exception as e: print(f"Error retrieving revision information: {e}") return None, None # Function to download Wikipedia page content def download_wikipedia_page(url, file_path): """Download the content of a Wikipedia page at the specified URL""" try: print(f"Downloading page content from: {url}") headers = {'User-Agent': 'WikipediaNavigationResearch/1.0 (research project)'} response = requests.get(url, headers=headers) response.raise_for_status() with open(file_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as file: file.write(response.text) print(f"Downloaded page content saved to: {file_path}") return response.text except Exception as e: print(f"Error downloading page: {e}") return None # Function to parse Wikipedia page and extract links def extract_links_from_html(html_content): """Extract internal Wikipedia links from HTML content""" soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser') # Find the main content area (typically in div with id 'mw-content-text') content_div = soup.find('div', id='mw-content-text') if not content_div: print("Could not find main content area in the page") return [] # Extract all links from the content area links = [] for a_tag in content_div.find_all('a', href=True): href = a_tag['href'] # Only include internal Wikipedia article links if href.startswith('/wiki/') and ':' not in href: title = href.replace('/wiki/', '') link_text = a_tag.get_text(strip=True) links.append({ 'title': title, 'text': link_text, 'href': href }) return links # Function to extract overview text from page def extract_page_overview(html_content): """Extract the first paragraph as an overview of the page""" soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser') # Find the main content area content_div = soup.find('div', id='mw-content-text') if not content_div: return "Overview extraction failed" # Find the first non-empty paragraph that's not inside a table or infobox for p in content_div.find_all('p'): if p.parent.name != 'td' and not p.find_previous('table', class_='infobox'): text = p.get_text(strip=True) if text and len(text) > 50: # Ensure it's a substantial paragraph return text return "No overview found" # Function to find common links between two pages def find_common_links(links1, links2): """Find common links between two sets of links""" # Create dictionaries for O(1) lookup links1_dict = {link['title']: link for link in links1} links2_dict = {link['title']: link for link in links2} # Find common titles common_titles = set(links1_dict.keys()) & set(links2_dict.keys()) # Create list of common links with data from links1 common_links = [links1_dict[title] for title in common_titles] return common_links # Function to analyze direct links between pages def analyze_direct_links(links1, links2, title1, title2): """Check if there are direct links between the two pages""" direct_links = { f"{title1}_to_{title2}": any(link['title'] == title2 for link in links1), f"{title2}_to_{title1}": any(link['title'] == title1 for link in links2) } return direct_links # Function to create network visualization def create_navigation_visualization(lotr_title, asoiaf_title, direct_links, common_links, categories): """Create and save a visualization of navigation paths""" print("\nCreating navigation visualization...") G = nx.DiGraph() # Add main nodes (the two pages) G.add_node(lotr_title, type='main', label='The Lord of the Rings') G.add_node(asoiaf_title, type='main', label='A Song of Ice and Fire') # Add direct links if they exist if direct_links.get(f"{lotr_title}_to_{asoiaf_title}"): G.add_edge(lotr_title, asoiaf_title, weight=2.0, type='direct') if direct_links.get(f"{asoiaf_title}_to_{lotr_title}"): G.add_edge(asoiaf_title, lotr_title, weight=2.0, type='direct') # Add top common links (limit to 15 for readability) top_links = common_links[:min(15, len(common_links))] for link in top_links: title = link['title'] G.add_node(title, type='common', label=link['text']) # Add edges from both main pages to this common link G.add_edge(lotr_title, title, weight=1.0) G.add_edge(asoiaf_title, title, weight=1.0) # Create the visualization plt.figure(figsize=(12, 10)) # Define node colors node_colors = [] node_sizes = [] for node in G.nodes(): if G.nodes[node]['type'] == 'main': node_colors.append('lightblue' if node == lotr_title else 'lightgreen') node_sizes.append(1500) else: # Color common links by category category = next((cat for cat, links in categories.items() if any(link['title'] == node for link in links)), 'Other') # Map categories to colors color_map = { 'Authors': 'orange', 'Genres': 'purple', 'Media Adaptations': 'pink', 'References & Identifiers': 'gray', 'Characters & Creatures': 'brown', 'Other': 'lightgray' } node_colors.append(color_map.get(category, 'lightgray')) node_sizes.append(800) # Position nodes using spring layout pos = nx.spring_layout(G, seed=42, k=0.5) # Draw nodes nx.draw_networkx_nodes(G, pos, node_color=node_colors, node_size=node_sizes, alpha=0.8) # Draw edges # Use different colors for direct vs. common links edge_colors = ['red' if G.edges[u, v].get('type') == 'direct' else 'gray' for u, v in G.edges()] nx.draw_networkx_edges(G, pos, width=1.5, edge_color=edge_colors, alpha=0.7, arrowsize=15, connectionstyle='arc3,rad=0.1') # Create node labels (use the 'label' attribute for display) labels = {node: G.nodes[node]['label'] if 'label' in G.nodes[node] else node for node in G.nodes()} # Draw labels with smaller font for common links main_nodes = [n for n in G.nodes() if G.nodes[n]['type'] == 'main'] common_nodes = [n for n in G.nodes() if G.nodes[n]['type'] == 'common'] # Draw main node labels nx.draw_networkx_labels(G, pos, labels={n: labels[n] for n in main_nodes}, font_size=12, font_weight='bold') # Draw common link labels with smaller font nx.draw_networkx_labels(G, pos, labels={n: labels[n] for n in common_nodes}, font_size=8) plt.title('Navigation Paths Between The Lord of the Rings and A Song of Ice and Fire\n(Wikipedia as of July 3, 2023)', fontsize=14) plt.axis('off') # Add a legend legend_elements = [ plt.Line2D([0], [0], marker='o', color='w', markerfacecolor='lightblue', markersize=15, label='The Lord of the Rings'), plt.Line2D([0], [0], marker='o', color='w', markerfacecolor='lightgreen', markersize=15, label='A Song of Ice and Fire'), ] # Add category colors to legend for category, color in { 'Authors': 'orange', 'Genres': 'purple', 'Media Adaptations': 'pink', 'Characters & Creatures': 'brown', 'References & Identifiers': 'gray', 'Other': 'lightgray' }.items(): if any(cat == category for cat in categories.keys()): legend_elements.append( plt.Line2D([0], [0], marker='o', color='w', markerfacecolor=color, markersize=10, label=category) ) # Add edge types to legend legend_elements.extend([ plt.Line2D([0], [0], color='red', lw=2, label='Direct Link'), plt.Line2D([0], [0], color='gray', lw=2, label='Common Link') ]) plt.legend(handles=legend_elements, loc='lower center', bbox_to_anchor=(0.5, -0.15), ncol=3, fontsize=10) # Save the visualization visualization_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'wikipedia_navigation_visualization.png') plt.tight_layout() plt.savefig(visualization_file, bbox_inches='tight', dpi=300) print(f"Visualization saved to: {visualization_file}") return visualization_file # Main execution function def main(): # Target date for the Wikipedia versions target_date = "2023-07-03" # Step 1: Define the Wikipedia page titles to analyze lotr_title = "The_Lord_of_the_Rings" asoiaf_title = "A_Song_of_Ice_and_Fire" print(f"\n=== ANALYZING WIKIPEDIA PAGES AS OF {target_date} ===") print(f"Pages to analyze: {lotr_title} and {asoiaf_title}\n") # Step 2: Get URLs for the specific versions on the target date lotr_url, lotr_revision = get_wikipedia_specific_version(lotr_title, target_date) asoiaf_url, asoiaf_revision = get_wikipedia_specific_version(asoiaf_title, target_date) if not lotr_url or not asoiaf_url: print("Failed to retrieve necessary revision information. Exiting.") return # Step 3: Download the page contents lotr_file_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, f"{lotr_title}_revision_{lotr_revision}.html") asoiaf_file_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, f"{asoiaf_title}_revision_{asoiaf_revision}.html") lotr_content = download_wikipedia_page(lotr_url, lotr_file_path) asoiaf_content = download_wikipedia_page(asoiaf_url, asoiaf_file_path) if not lotr_content or not asoiaf_content: print("Failed to download one or both page contents. Exiting.") return # Step 4: Extract links and overview from both pages print("\nExtracting links and content from both pages...") lotr_links = extract_links_from_html(lotr_content) asoiaf_links = extract_links_from_html(asoiaf_content) lotr_overview = extract_page_overview(lotr_content) asoiaf_overview = extract_page_overview(asoiaf_content) print(f"Found {len(lotr_links)} links in {lotr_title} page") print(f"Found {len(asoiaf_links)} links in {asoiaf_title} page") # Step 5: Analyze navigation paths # Check for direct links between pages direct_links = analyze_direct_links(lotr_links, asoiaf_links, lotr_title, asoiaf_title) print("\n=== DIRECT LINK ANALYSIS ===") for path, exists in direct_links.items(): status = "EXISTS" if exists else "DOES NOT EXIST" print(f"{path}: {status}") # Find common links (potential two-hop paths) common_links = find_common_links(lotr_links, asoiaf_links) print(f"\n=== COMMON LINKS ANALYSIS ===") print(f"Found {len(common_links)} common links (potential intermediate pages)") # Display a sample of common links print("\nSample of common links (potential intermediate pages):") for i, link in enumerate(common_links[:10], 1): print(f"{i}. {link['text']} (/wiki/{link['title']})") # Categorize common links print("\nCategorizing common links...") categories = defaultdict(list) # More comprehensive categorization based on keywords in titles and text for link in common_links: title = link['title'].lower() text = link['text'].lower() if any(keyword in title or keyword in text for keyword in ['tolkien', 'author', 'writer', 'martin', 'rowling']): categories['Authors'].append(link) elif any(keyword in title or keyword in text for keyword in ['fantasy', 'fiction', 'genre', 'epic']): categories['Genres'].append(link) elif any(keyword in title or keyword in text for keyword in ['film', 'movie', 'tv', 'television', 'adaptation', 'series', 'game']): categories['Media Adaptations'].append(link) elif any(keyword in title for keyword in ['identifier', 'isbn', 'oclc', 'doi']) or title.startswith('international_'): categories['References & Identifiers'].append(link) elif any(keyword in title or keyword in text for keyword in ['character', 'creature', 'people', 'race', 'orc', 'elf', 'dragon']): categories['Characters & Creatures'].append(link) elif any(keyword in title or keyword in text for keyword in ['world', 'universe', 'realm', 'land', 'setting', 'geography']): categories['World-Building'].append(link) elif any(keyword in title or keyword in text for keyword in ['magazine', 'journal', 'newspaper', 'publication', 'press']): categories['Publications'].append(link) elif any(keyword in title or keyword in text for keyword in ['mythology', 'legend', 'folklore', 'tale']): categories['Mythology & Folklore'].append(link) else: categories['Other'].append(link) # Print categorization results print("\nCommon links by category:") for category, links in categories.items(): print(f"{category}: {len(links)} links") # Print first 3 examples for each category for i, link in enumerate(links[:3], 1): if i <= 3: # Limit to first 3 examples print(f" {i}. {link['text']} (/wiki/{link['title']})") if len(links) > 3: print(f" ... and {len(links) - 3} more") # Step 6: Create visualization of navigation paths visualization_file = create_navigation_visualization( lotr_title, asoiaf_title, direct_links, common_links, categories) # Step 7: Save detailed analysis results to JSON results = { 'analysis_date': datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"), 'target_date': target_date, 'pages': { lotr_title: { 'title': 'The Lord of the Rings', 'revision_id': lotr_revision, 'revision_url': lotr_url, 'file': os.path.basename(lotr_file_path), 'link_count': len(lotr_links), 'overview': lotr_overview[:300] + '...' if len(lotr_overview) > 300 else lotr_overview }, asoiaf_title: { 'title': 'A Song of Ice and Fire', 'revision_id': asoiaf_revision, 'revision_url': asoiaf_url, 'file': os.path.basename(asoiaf_file_path), 'link_count': len(asoiaf_links), 'overview': asoiaf_overview[:300] + '...' if len(asoiaf_overview) > 300 else asoiaf_overview } }, 'navigation_paths': { 'direct_links': direct_links, 'common_links': [ { 'title': link['title'], 'text': link['text'], 'href': link['href'], 'category': next((cat for cat, links in categories.items() if link in links), 'Uncategorized') } for link in common_links ], 'common_links_by_category': { category: len(links) for category, links in categories.items() } }, 'summary': { 'direct_path_exists': any(direct_links.values()), 'direct_paths': [ path.replace('_to_', ' â†’ ').replace('_', ' ') for path, exists in direct_links.items() if exists ], 'intermediate_paths_count': len(common_links), 'top_intermediate_pages': [ { 'title': link['title'], 'text': link['text'], 'category': next((cat for cat, links in categories.items() if link in links), 'Uncategorized') } for link in common_links[:10] ], 'visualization_file': os.path.basename(visualization_file) } } # Save results to JSON file results_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'wikipedia_navigation_analysis.json') with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(results, f, indent=2) print(f"\nAnalysis results saved to: {results_file}") # Generate a summary report print("\n=== SUMMARY REPORT ===") print(f"Analysis of Wikipedia pages as of {target_date}:") print(f"1. {lotr_title}: {len(lotr_links)} internal links") print(f"2. {asoiaf_title}: {len(asoiaf_links)} internal links") if any(direct_links.values()): direct_paths = [path.replace('_to_', ' â†’ ').replace('_', ' ') for path, exists in direct_links.items() if exists] for i, path in enumerate(direct_paths, 1): print(f"3.{i} Direct link: {path}") else: print("3. No direct links between the pages") print(f"4. Found {len(common_links)} common links (potential intermediate pages)") print("5. Most promising intermediate pages:") for i, link in enumerate(common_links[:5], 1): category = next((cat for cat, links in categories.items() if link in links), 'Uncategorized') print(f" {i}. {link['text']} ({category})") # Execute the main function if __name__ == "__main__": main()

import os import requests import json from bs4 import BeautifulSoup from urllib.parse import urljoin, quote from datetime import datetime import networkx as nx import matplotlib.pyplot as plt from collections import defaultdict def create_directory_if_not_exists(directory): """Create a directory if it doesn't exist""" if not os.path.exists(directory): os.makedirs(directory) return directory # Create workspace directory workspace_dir = 'workspace' create_directory_if_not_exists(workspace_dir) # Function to get a specific Wikipedia page version on a date def get_wikipedia_specific_version(title, date_str): """Get the version of a Wikipedia page as it existed on the specified date""" print(f"Retrieving Wikipedia page for '{title}' as it appeared on {date_str}...") # Convert date format from YYYY-MM-DD to YYYYMMDD for API date_formatted = date_str.replace('-', '') # Step 1: Use the MediaWiki API to find the revision closest to the target date api_url = f"https://en.wikipedia.org/w/api.php" params = { 'action': 'query', 'prop': 'revisions', 'titles': title, 'rvlimit': 1, 'rvprop': 'ids|timestamp', 'rvstart': f"{date_formatted}000000", # Start of the day in format YYYYMMDDHHMMSS 'format': 'json' } try: print(f"Querying Wikipedia API for revision ID on {date_str}...") headers = {'User-Agent': 'WikipediaNavigationResearch/1.0 (research project)'} response = requests.get(api_url, params=params, headers=headers) response.raise_for_status() # Raise an exception for HTTP errors data = response.json() # Extract revision ID from the API response pages = data.get('query', {}).get('pages', {}) if not pages: print(f"No page data returned for {title}") return None, None page_id = next(iter(pages.keys())) page_data = pages[page_id] if page_id == '-1' or 'missing' in page_data: print(f"Page {title} not found") return None, None revisions = page_data.get('revisions', []) if not revisions: print(f"No revisions found for {title} on or before {date_str}") return None, None revision = revisions[0] revision_id = revision.get('revid') timestamp = revision.get('timestamp') print(f"Found revision {revision_id} from {timestamp}") # Step 2: Construct the URL for the specific revision encoded_title = quote(title) revision_url = f"https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title={encoded_title}&oldid={revision_id}" return revision_url, revision_id except Exception as e: print(f"Error retrieving revision information: {e}") return None, None # Function to download Wikipedia page content def download_wikipedia_page(url, file_path): """Download the content of a Wikipedia page at the specified URL""" try: print(f"Downloading page content from: {url}") headers = {'User-Agent': 'WikipediaNavigationResearch/1.0 (research project)'} response = requests.get(url, headers=headers) response.raise_for_status() with open(file_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as file: file.write(response.text) print(f"Downloaded page content saved to: {file_path}") return response.text except Exception as e: print(f"Error downloading page: {e}") return None # Function to parse Wikipedia page and extract links def extract_links_from_html(html_content): """Extract internal Wikipedia links from HTML content""" soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser') # Find the main content area (typically in div with id 'mw-content-text') content_div = soup.find('div', id='mw-content-text') if not content_div: print("Could not find main content area in the page") return [] # Extract all links from the content area links = [] for a_tag in content_div.find_all('a', href=True): href = a_tag['href'] # Only include internal Wikipedia article links if href.startswith('/wiki/') and ':' not in href: title = href.replace('/wiki/', '') link_text = a_tag.get_text(strip=True) links.append({ 'title': title, 'text': link_text, 'href': href }) return links # Function to extract overview text from page def extract_page_overview(html_content): """Extract the first paragraph as an overview of the page""" soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser') # Find the main content area content_div = soup.find('div', id='mw-content-text') if not content_div: return "Overview extraction failed" # Find the first non-empty paragraph that's not inside a table or infobox for p in content_div.find_all('p'): if p.parent.name != 'td' and not p.find_previous('table', class_='infobox'): text = p.get_text(strip=True) if text and len(text) > 50: # Ensure it's a substantial paragraph return text return "No overview found" # Function to find common links between two pages def find_common_links(links1, links2): """Find common links between two sets of links""" # Create dictionaries for O(1) lookup links1_dict = {link['title']: link for link in links1} links2_dict = {link['title']: link for link in links2} # Find common titles common_titles = set(links1_dict.keys()) & set(links2_dict.keys()) # Create list of common links with data from links1 common_links = [links1_dict[title] for title in common_titles] return common_links # Function to analyze direct links between pages def analyze_direct_links(links1, links2, title1, title2): """Check if there are direct links between the two pages""" direct_links = { f"{title1}_to_{title2}": any(link['title'] == title2 for link in links1), f"{title2}_to_{title1}": any(link['title'] == title1 for link in links2) } return direct_links # Function to create network visualization def create_navigation_visualization(lotr_title, asoiaf_title, direct_links, common_links, categories): """Create and save a visualization of navigation paths""" print("\nCreating navigation visualization...") G = nx.DiGraph() # Add main nodes (the two pages) G.add_node(lotr_title, type='main', label='The Lord of the Rings') G.add_node(asoiaf_title, type='main', label='A Song of Ice and Fire') # Add direct links if they exist if direct_links.get(f"{lotr_title}_to_{asoiaf_title}"): G.add_edge(lotr_title, asoiaf_title, weight=2.0, type='direct') if direct_links.get(f"{asoiaf_title}_to_{lotr_title}"): G.add_edge(asoiaf_title, lotr_title, weight=2.0, type='direct') # Add top common links (limit to 15 for readability) top_links = common_links[:min(15, len(common_links))] for link in top_links: title = link['title'] G.add_node(title, type='common', label=link['text']) # Add edges from both main pages to this common link G.add_edge(lotr_title, title, weight=1.0) G.add_edge(asoiaf_title, title, weight=1.0) # Create the visualization plt.figure(figsize=(12, 10)) # Define node colors node_colors = [] node_sizes = [] for node in G.nodes(): if G.nodes[node]['type'] == 'main': node_colors.append('lightblue' if node == lotr_title else 'lightgreen') node_sizes.append(1500) else: # Color common links by category category = next((cat for cat, links in categories.items() if any(link['title'] == node for link in links)), 'Other') # Map categories to colors color_map = { 'Authors': 'orange', 'Genres': 'purple', 'Media Adaptations': 'pink', 'References & Identifiers': 'gray', 'Characters & Creatures': 'brown', 'Other': 'lightgray' } node_colors.append(color_map.get(category, 'lightgray')) node_sizes.append(800) # Position nodes using spring layout pos = nx.spring_layout(G, seed=42, k=0.5) # Draw nodes nx.draw_networkx_nodes(G, pos, node_color=node_colors, node_size=node_sizes, alpha=0.8) # Draw edges # Use different colors for direct vs. common links edge_colors = ['red' if G.edges[u, v].get('type') == 'direct' else 'gray' for u, v in G.edges()] nx.draw_networkx_edges(G, pos, width=1.5, edge_color=edge_colors, alpha=0.7, arrowsize=15, connectionstyle='arc3,rad=0.1') # Create node labels (use the 'label' attribute for display) labels = {node: G.nodes[node]['label'] if 'label' in G.nodes[node] else node for node in G.nodes()} # Draw labels with smaller font for common links main_nodes = [n for n in G.nodes() if G.nodes[n]['type'] == 'main'] common_nodes = [n for n in G.nodes() if G.nodes[n]['type'] == 'common'] # Draw main node labels nx.draw_networkx_labels(G, pos, labels={n: labels[n] for n in main_nodes}, font_size=12, font_weight='bold') # Draw common link labels with smaller font nx.draw_networkx_labels(G, pos, labels={n: labels[n] for n in common_nodes}, font_size=8) plt.title('Navigation Paths Between The Lord of the Rings and A Song of Ice and Fire\n(Wikipedia as of July 3, 2023)', fontsize=14) plt.axis('off') # Add a legend legend_elements = [ plt.Line2D([0], [0], marker='o', color='w', markerfacecolor='lightblue', markersize=15, label='The Lord of the Rings'), plt.Line2D([0], [0], marker='o', color='w', markerfacecolor='lightgreen', markersize=15, label='A Song of Ice and Fire'), ] # Add category colors to legend for category, color in { 'Authors': 'orange', 'Genres': 'purple', 'Media Adaptations': 'pink', 'Characters & Creatures': 'brown', 'References & Identifiers': 'gray', 'Other': 'lightgray' }.items(): if any(cat == category for cat in categories.keys()): legend_elements.append( plt.Line2D([0], [0], marker='o', color='w', markerfacecolor=color, markersize=10, label=category) ) # Add edge types to legend legend_elements.extend([ plt.Line2D([0], [0], color='red', lw=2, label='Direct Link'), plt.Line2D([0], [0], color='gray', lw=2, label='Common Link') ]) plt.legend(handles=legend_elements, loc='lower center', bbox_to_anchor=(0.5, -0.15), ncol=3, fontsize=10) # Save the visualization visualization_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'wikipedia_navigation_visualization.png') plt.tight_layout() plt.savefig(visualization_file, bbox_inches='tight', dpi=300) print(f"Visualization saved to: {visualization_file}") return visualization_file # Main execution function def main(): # Target date for the Wikipedia versions target_date = "2023-07-03" # Step 1: Define the Wikipedia page titles to analyze lotr_title = "The_Lord_of_the_Rings" asoiaf_title = "A_Song_of_Ice_and_Fire" print(f"\n=== ANALYZING WIKIPEDIA PAGES AS OF {target_date} ===") print(f"Pages to analyze: {lotr_title} and {asoiaf_title}\n") # Step 2: Get URLs for the specific versions on the target date lotr_url, lotr_revision = get_wikipedia_specific_version(lotr_title, target_date) asoiaf_url, asoiaf_revision = get_wikipedia_specific_version(asoiaf_title, target_date) if not lotr_url or not asoiaf_url: print("Failed to retrieve necessary revision information. Exiting.") return # Step 3: Download the page contents lotr_file_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, f"{lotr_title}_revision_{lotr_revision}.html") asoiaf_file_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, f"{asoiaf_title}_revision_{asoiaf_revision}.html") lotr_content = download_wikipedia_page(lotr_url, lotr_file_path) asoiaf_content = download_wikipedia_page(asoiaf_url, asoiaf_file_path) if not lotr_content or not asoiaf_content: print("Failed to download one or both page contents. Exiting.") return # Step 4: Extract links and overview from both pages print("\nExtracting links and content from both pages...") lotr_links = extract_links_from_html(lotr_content) asoiaf_links = extract_links_from_html(asoiaf_content) lotr_overview = extract_page_overview(lotr_content) asoiaf_overview = extract_page_overview(asoiaf_content) print(f"Found {len(lotr_links)} links in {lotr_title} page") print(f"Found {len(asoiaf_links)} links in {asoiaf_title} page") # Step 5: Analyze navigation paths # Check for direct links between pages direct_links = analyze_direct_links(lotr_links, asoiaf_links, lotr_title, asoiaf_title) print("\n=== DIRECT LINK ANALYSIS ===") for path, exists in direct_links.items(): status = "EXISTS" if exists else "DOES NOT EXIST" print(f"{path}: {status}") # Find common links (potential two-hop paths) common_links = find_common_links(lotr_links, asoiaf_links) print(f"\n=== COMMON LINKS ANALYSIS ===") print(f"Found {len(common_links)} common links (potential intermediate pages)") # Display a sample of common links print("\nSample of common links (potential intermediate pages):") for i, link in enumerate(common_links[:10], 1): print(f"{i}. {link['text']} (/wiki/{link['title']})") # Categorize common links print("\nCategorizing common links...") categories = defaultdict(list) # More comprehensive categorization based on keywords in titles and text for link in common_links: title = link['title'].lower() text = link['text'].lower() if any(keyword in title or keyword in text for keyword in ['tolkien', 'author', 'writer', 'martin', 'rowling']): categories['Authors'].append(link) elif any(keyword in title or keyword in text for keyword in ['fantasy', 'fiction', 'genre', 'epic']): categories['Genres'].append(link) elif any(keyword in title or keyword in text for keyword in ['film', 'movie', 'tv', 'television', 'adaptation', 'series', 'game']): categories['Media Adaptations'].append(link) elif any(keyword in title for keyword in ['identifier', 'isbn', 'oclc', 'doi']) or title.startswith('international_'): categories['References & Identifiers'].append(link) elif any(keyword in title or keyword in text for keyword in ['character', 'creature', 'people', 'race', 'orc', 'elf', 'dragon']): categories['Characters & Creatures'].append(link) elif any(keyword in title or keyword in text for keyword in ['world', 'universe', 'realm', 'land', 'setting', 'geography']): categories['World-Building'].append(link) elif any(keyword in title or keyword in text for keyword in ['magazine', 'journal', 'newspaper', 'publication', 'press']): categories['Publications'].append(link) elif any(keyword in title or keyword in text for keyword in ['mythology', 'legend', 'folklore', 'tale']): categories['Mythology & Folklore'].append(link) else: categories['Other'].append(link) # Print categorization results print("\nCommon links by category:") for category, links in categories.items(): print(f"{category}: {len(links)} links") # Print first 3 examples for each category for i, link in enumerate(links[:3], 1): if i <= 3: # Limit to first 3 examples print(f" {i}. {link['text']} (/wiki/{link['title']})") if len(links) > 3: print(f" ... and {len(links) - 3} more") # Step 6: Create visualization of navigation paths visualization_file = create_navigation_visualization( lotr_title, asoiaf_title, direct_links, common_links, categories) # Step 7: Save detailed analysis results to JSON results = { 'analysis_date': datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"), 'target_date': target_date, 'pages': { lotr_title: { 'title': 'The Lord of the Rings', 'revision_id': lotr_revision, 'revision_url': lotr_url, 'file': os.path.basename(lotr_file_path), 'link_count': len(lotr_links), 'overview': lotr_overview[:300] + '...' if len(lotr_overview) > 300 else lotr_overview }, asoiaf_title: { 'title': 'A Song of Ice and Fire', 'revision_id': asoiaf_revision, 'revision_url': asoiaf_url, 'file': os.path.basename(asoiaf_file_path), 'link_count': len(asoiaf_links), 'overview': asoiaf_overview[:300] + '...' if len(asoiaf_overview) > 300 else asoiaf_overview } }, 'navigation_paths': { 'direct_links': direct_links, 'common_links': [ { 'title': link['title'], 'text': link['text'], 'href': link['href'], 'category': next((cat for cat, links in categories.items() if link in links), 'Uncategorized') } for link in common_links ], 'common_links_by_category': { category: len(links) for category, links in categories.items() } }, 'summary': { 'direct_path_exists': any(direct_links.values()), 'direct_paths': [ path.replace('_to_', ' â†’ ').replace('_', ' ') for path, exists in direct_links.items() if exists ], 'intermediate_paths_count': len(common_links), 'top_intermediate_pages': [ { 'title': link['title'], 'text': link['text'], 'category': next((cat for cat, links in categories.items() if link in links), 'Uncategorized') } for link in common_links[:10] ], 'visualization_file': os.path.basename(visualization_file) } } # Save results to JSON file results_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'wikipedia_navigation_analysis.json') with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(results, f, indent=2) print(f"\nAnalysis results saved to: {results_file}") # No direct links between the pages") print(f"4. Found {len(common_links)} common links (potential intermediate pages)") print("5. Most promising intermediate pages:") for i, link in enumerate(common_links[:5], 1): category = next((cat for cat, links in categories.items() if link in links), 'Uncategorized') print(f" {i}. {link['text']} ({category})") # Execute the main function if __name__ == "__main__": main()

import os import json import networkx as nx def inspect_file(file_path): """Inspect a file's content and structure""" print(f"Inspecting file: {file_path}") try: with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: content = f.read() # Try to parse as JSON try: data = json.loads(content) print(f"File is JSON formatted") print(f"Top-level structure: {type(data)}") if isinstance(data, dict): print(f"Keys: {list(data.keys())}") for key, value in data.items(): value_type = type(value) preview = str(value)[:100] + '...' if len(str(value)) > 100 else str(value) print(f" - {key} ({value_type}): {preview}") # If it's a list or dict, show more details if isinstance(value, list) and value: print(f" List length: {len(value)}") if value: print(f" First item type: {type(value[0])}") if isinstance(value[0], dict): print(f" First item keys: {list(value[0].keys())}") elif isinstance(value, dict): print(f" Dict keys: {list(value.keys())}") elif isinstance(data, list): print(f"List with {len(data)} items") if data: print(f"First item type: {type(data[0])}") if isinstance(data[0], dict): print(f"First item keys: {list(data[0].keys())}") preview = str(data[0])[:100] + '...' if len(str(data[0])) > 100 else str(data[0]) print(f"First item: {preview}") return data except json.JSONDecodeError: print("File is not JSON formatted. Showing as text:") print(content[:500] + '...' if len(content) > 500 else content) return content except Exception as e: print(f"Error reading file: {e}") return None # First, check the workspace directory to see what files we have workspace_dir = 'workspace' print(f"Checking contents of {workspace_dir} directory:") files = [] if os.path.exists(workspace_dir): files = os.listdir(workspace_dir) for file in files: file_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, file) if os.path.isfile(file_path): print(f" - {file} ({os.path.getsize(file_path)} bytes)") else: print(f" Directory {workspace_dir} does not exist") # Look for Wikipedia data files that might contain our source and target pages wiki_files = [file for file in files if 'wiki' in file.lower() or 'lord' in file.lower() or 'rings' in file.lower() or 'ice' in file.lower() or 'fire' in file.lower() or 'song' in file.lower()] print(f"\nPotential Wikipedia data files: {wiki_files}") # Load and analyze each potential file wiki_data = {} for file in wiki_files: file_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, file) print(f"\n{'='*50}") data = inspect_file(file_path) if data: wiki_data[file] = data # If no existing files are found, we need to report that we need to retrieve the data if not wiki_data: print("\nNo Wikipedia data files found. We need to retrieve the page content first.") print("Let's try to read these Wikipedia pages and analyze their links:") print("1. 'The Lord of the Rings' (source)") print("2. 'A Song of Ice and Fire' (target)") import requests from bs4 import BeautifulSoup # Function to fetch Wikipedia page and extract links def get_wiki_page_links(title): url = f"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/{title.replace(' ', '_')}" print(f"Fetching: {url}") try: response = requests.get(url, timeout=10) response.raise_for_status() soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser') # Extract page title page_title = soup.find('h1', {'id': 'firstHeading'}).text.strip() print(f"Page title: {page_title}") # Extract links from the main content content_div = soup.find('div', {'id': 'mw-content-text'}) if not content_div: print("Could not find content div") return None # Get all links from the content area links = [] for a in content_div.find_all('a', href=True): href = a['href'] # Only include internal wiki links if href.startswith('/wiki/') and ':' not in href: # Extract the page title from the link link_title = href.replace('/wiki/', '').replace('_', ' ') links.append(link_title) print(f"Found {len(links)} internal links") return { 'title': page_title, 'url': url, 'links': links } except Exception as e: print(f"Error fetching {url}: {e}") return None # Get data for both pages source_page = "The_Lord_of_the_Rings" target_page = "A_Song_of_Ice_and_Fire" source_data = get_wiki_page_links(source_page) target_data = get_wiki_page_links(target_page) # Save the data for future use if source_data: with open(os.path.join(workspace_dir, f"{source_page}_data.json"), 'w') as f: json.dump(source_data, f, indent=2) print(f"Saved source page data to {source_page}_data.json") if target_data: with open(os.path.join(workspace_dir, f"{target_page}_data.json"), 'w') as f: json.dump(target_data, f, indent=2) print(f"Saved target page data to {target_page}_data.json") # Reload the file list files = os.listdir(workspace_dir) wiki_files = [file for file in files if 'wiki' in file.lower() or 'lord' in file.lower() or 'rings' in file.lower() or 'ice' in file.lower() or 'fire' in file.lower() or 'song' in file.lower()] for file in wiki_files: file_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, file) print(f"\n{'='*50}") data = inspect_file(file_path) if data: wiki_data[file] = data # Now let's analyze the data to find the minimum click path print("\n" + "="*50) print("ANALYZING CLICK PATH") print("="*50) # Extract source and target page data source_data = None target_data = None source_page = "The Lord of the Rings" target_page = "A Song of Ice and Fire" # Try to find data for our source and target pages for filename, data in wiki_data.items(): if isinstance(data, dict) and 'title' in data: if data['title'] == source_page or source_page.lower() in data['title'].lower() or source_page.replace('_', ' ').lower() in data['title'].lower(): source_data = data print(f"Found source page data in {filename}") elif data['title'] == target_page or target_page.lower() in data['title'].lower() or target_page.replace('_', ' ').lower() in data['title'].lower(): target_data = data print(f"Found target page data in {filename}") # If we still don't have the required data, explore other data structures if not (source_data and target_data): for filename, data in wiki_data.items(): if isinstance(data, dict): for key, value in data.items(): if isinstance(value, dict): if 'title' in value and (value['title'] == source_page or source_page.lower() in value['title'].lower() or source_page.replace('_', ' ').lower() in value['title'].lower()): source_data = value print(f"Found source page data in {filename} -> {key}") elif 'title' in value and (value['title'] == target_page or target_page.lower() in value['title'].lower() or target_page.replace('_', ' ').lower() in value['title'].lower()): target_data = value print(f"Found target page data in {filename} -> {key}") # Check if we have both source and target data if source_data and target_data: print(f"\nSource page: {source_data['title']}") print(f"Target page: {target_data['title']}") # Direct link check direct_link = False if 'links' in source_data and target_data['title'] in source_data['links']: direct_link = True print(f"\nDirect link found from {source_data['title']} to {target_data['title']}") print("Minimum click path length: 1") elif 'links' in source_data: target_variations = [target_data['title'], target_data['title'].lower(), target_page, target_page.lower(), target_page.replace('_', ' '), target_page.replace('_', ' ').lower()] for link in source_data['links']: if link in target_variations or any(tv in link.lower() for tv in target_variations): direct_link = True print(f"\nDirect link found from {source_data['title']} to {target_data['title']} (matching: {link})") print("Minimum click path length: 1") break if not direct_link: print(f"\nNo direct link from {source_data['title']} to {target_data['title']}") print("Need to explore indirect paths...") # Build a graph of the known Wikipedia links graph = nx.DiGraph() # Add nodes and edges for source page source_normalized = source_data['title'].lower().replace(' ', '_') graph.add_node(source_normalized) target_normalized = target_data['title'].lower().replace(' ', '_') graph.add_node(target_normalized) if 'links' in source_data: for link in source_data['links']: link_normalized = link.lower().replace(' ', '_') graph.add_node(link_normalized) graph.add_edge(source_normalized, link_normalized) # Add nodes and edges for target page if 'links' in target_data: for link in target_data['links']: link_normalized = link.lower().replace(' ', '_') graph.add_node(link_normalized) graph.add_edge(target_normalized, link_normalized) # Check for common links (two-click path) common_links = set() if 'links' in source_data and 'links' in target_data: source_links = {link.lower().replace(' ', '_') for link in source_data['links']} target_links = {link.lower().replace(' ', '_') for link in target_data['links']} common_links = source_links.intersection(target_links) if common_links: print(f"\nFound {len(common_links)} common links between source and target:") for i, link in enumerate(sorted(common_links)[:10]): # Show first 10 common links print(f" {i+1}. {link.replace('_', ' ')}") if len(common_links) > 10: print(f" ... and {len(common_links) - 10} more") print("\nMinimum click path length: 2") print(f"Path: {source_data['title']} -> [any common link] -> {target_data['title']}") else: print("\nNo common links found between source and target pages.") print("Need more data or a breadth-first search to find the shortest path.") print("This would require fetching additional Wikipedia pages.") # Try to find a path with the data we have try: if nx.has_path(graph, source_normalized, target_normalized): shortest_path = nx.shortest_path(graph, source_normalized, target_normalized) print(f"\nFound a path in our current graph: {shortest_path}") print(f"Minimum click path length: {len(shortest_path)-1}") else: reverse_path = nx.shortest_path(graph, target_normalized, source_normalized) if nx.has_path(graph, target_normalized, source_normalized) else None if reverse_path: print(f"\nFound a reverse path (target to source): {reverse_path}") print(f"Reverse path length: {len(reverse_path)-1}") else: print("\nCurrent graph does not have a complete path between source and target.") print("We would need to explore more pages to find the complete path.") except nx.NetworkXNoPath: print("\nNo path found in our current graph.") else: print("\nMissing link data for one or both pages.") print("Need to collect more data to determine the click path.") else: print("\nMissing data for one or both pages. Cannot analyze the click path.") print(f"Have source page data: {source_data is not None}") print(f"Have target page data: {target_data is not None}") # If we don't have the data, suggest what we need to do if not (source_data or target_data): print("\nWe need to fetch both Wikipedia pages to analyze the click path:") print(f"1. {source_page}") print(f"2. {target_page}") elif not source_data: print(f"\nWe need to fetch the source page: {source_page}") else: print(f"\nWe need to fetch the target page: {target_page}") print("\nCOMPLETE ANALYSIS SUMMARY:") print("=" * 50) if source_data and target_data: if direct_link: print(f"A direct link exists from '{source_page}' to '{target_page}'") print("Minimum click path length: 1") elif 'links' in source_data and 'links' in target_data and common_links: print(f"No direct link, but {len(common_links)} common links found") print("Minimum click path length: 2") print(f"Example path: {source_page} -> {list(common_links)[0].replace('_', ' ')} -> {target_page}") else: print("No direct link or common link found with current data") print("Would need to explore more pages to determine exact path length") else: print("Insufficient data to determine the minimum click path") print("Need to fetch Wikipedia page content for analysis")

import os import json import networkx as nx def inspect_file(file_path): """Inspect a file's content and structure""" print(f"Inspecting file: {file_path}") try: with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: content = f.read() # Try to parse as JSON try: data = json.loads(content) print(f"File is JSON formatted") print(f"Top-level structure: {type(data)}") if isinstance(data, dict): print(f"Keys: {list(data.keys())}") for key, value in data.items(): value_type = type(value) preview = str(value)[:100] + '...' if len(str(value)) > 100 else str(value) print(f" - {key} ({value_type}): {preview}") # If it's a list or dict, show more details if isinstance(value, list) and value: print(f" List length: {len(value)}") if value: print(f" First item type: {type(value[0])}") if isinstance(value[0], dict): print(f" First item keys: {list(value[0].keys())}") elif isinstance(value, dict): print(f" Dict keys: {list(value.keys())}") elif isinstance(data, list): print(f"List with {len(data)} items") if data: print(f"First item type: {type(data[0])}") if isinstance(data[0], dict): print(f"First item keys: {list(data[0].keys())}") preview = str(data[0])[:100] + '...' if len(str(data[0])) > 100 else str(data[0]) print(f"First item: {preview}") return data except json.JSONDecodeError: print("File is not JSON formatted. Showing as text:") print(content[:500] + '...' if len(content) > 500 else content) return content except Exception as e: print(f"Error reading file: {e}") return None # First, check the workspace directory to see what files we have workspace_dir = 'workspace' print(f"Checking contents of {workspace_dir} directory:") files = [] if os.path.exists(workspace_dir): files = os.listdir(workspace_dir) for file in files: file_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, file) if os.path.isfile(file_path): print(f" - {file} ({os.path.getsize(file_path)} bytes)") else: print(f" Directory {workspace_dir} does not exist") # Look for Wikipedia data files that might contain our source and target pages wiki_files = [file for file in files if 'wiki' in file.lower() or 'lord' in file.lower() or 'rings' in file.lower() or 'ice' in file.lower() or 'fire' in file.lower() or 'song' in file.lower()] print(f"\nPotential Wikipedia data files: {wiki_files}") # Load and analyze each potential file wiki_data = {} for file in wiki_files: file_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, file) print(f"\n{'='*50}") data = inspect_file(file_path) if data: wiki_data[file] = data # If no existing files are found, we need to report that we need to retrieve the data if not wiki_data: print("\nNo Wikipedia data files found. We need to retrieve the page content first.") print("Let's try to read these Wikipedia pages and analyze their links:") print("1. 'The Lord of the Rings' (source)") print("2. 'A Song of Ice and Fire' (target)") import requests from bs4 import BeautifulSoup # Function to fetch Wikipedia page and extract links def get_wiki_page_links(title): url = f"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/{title.replace(' ', '_')}" print(f"Fetching: {url}") try: response = requests.get(url, timeout=10) response.raise_for_status() soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser') # Extract page title page_title = soup.find('h1', {'id': 'firstHeading'}).text.strip() print(f"Page title: {page_title}") # Extract links from the main content content_div = soup.find('div', {'id': 'mw-content-text'}) if not content_div: print("Could not find content div") return None # Get all links from the content area links = [] for a in content_div.find_all('a', href=True): href = a['href'] # Only include internal wiki links if href.startswith('/wiki/') and ':' not in href: # Extract the page title from the link link_title = href.replace('/wiki/', '').replace('_', ' ') links.append(link_title) print(f"Found {len(links)} internal links") return { 'title': page_title, 'url': url, 'links': links } except Exception as e: print(f"Error fetching {url}: {e}") return None # Get data for both pages source_page = "The_Lord_of_the_Rings" target_page = "A_Song_of_Ice_and_Fire" source_data = get_wiki_page_links(source_page) target_data = get_wiki_page_links(target_page) # Save the data for future use if source_data: with open(os.path.join(workspace_dir, f"{source_page}_data.json"), 'w') as f: json.dump(source_data, f, indent=2) print(f"Saved source page data to {source_page}_data.json") if target_data: with open(os.path.join(workspace_dir, f"{target_page}_data.json"), 'w') as f: json.dump(target_data, f, indent=2) print(f"Saved target page data to {target_page}_data.json") # Reload the file list files = os.listdir(workspace_dir) wiki_files = [file for file in files if 'wiki' in file.lower() or 'lord' in file.lower() or 'rings' in file.lower() or 'ice' in file.lower() or 'fire' in file.lower() or 'song' in file.lower()] for file in wiki_files: file_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, file) print(f"\n{'='*50}") data = inspect_file(file_path) if data: wiki_data[file] = data # Now let's analyze the data to find the minimum click path print("\n" + "="*50) print("ANALYZING CLICK PATH") print("="*50) # Extract source and target page data source_data = None target_data = None source_page = "The Lord of the Rings" target_page = "A Song of Ice and Fire" # Try to find data for our source and target pages for filename, data in wiki_data.items(): if isinstance(data, dict) and 'title' in data: if data['title'] == source_page or source_page.lower() in data['title'].lower() or source_page.replace('_', ' ').lower() in data['title'].lower(): source_data = data print(f"Found source page data in {filename}") elif data['title'] == target_page or target_page.lower() in data['title'].lower() or target_page.replace('_', ' ').lower() in data['title'].lower(): target_data = data print(f"Found target page data in {filename}") # If we still don't have the required data, explore other data structures if not (source_data and target_data): for filename, data in wiki_data.items(): if isinstance(data, dict): for key, value in data.items(): if isinstance(value, dict): if 'title' in value and (value['title'] == source_page or source_page.lower() in value['title'].lower() or source_page.replace('_', ' ').lower() in value['title'].lower()): source_data = value print(f"Found source page data in {filename} -> {key}") elif 'title' in value and (value['title'] == target_page or target_page.lower() in value['title'].lower() or target_page.replace('_', ' ').lower() in value['title'].lower()): target_data = value print(f"Found target page data in {filename} -> {key}") # Check if we have both source and target data if source_data and target_data: print(f"\nSource page: {source_data['title']}") print(f"Target page: {target_data['title']}") # Direct link check direct_link = False if 'links' in source_data and target_data['title'] in source_data['links']: direct_link = True print(f"\nDirect link found from {source_data['title']} to {target_data['title']}") print("Minimum click path length: 1") elif 'links' in source_data: target_variations = [target_data['title'], target_data['title'].lower(), target_page, target_page.lower(), target_page.replace('_', ' '), target_page.replace('_', ' ').lower()] for link in source_data['links']: if link in target_variations or any(tv in link.lower() for tv in target_variations): direct_link = True print(f"\nDirect link found from {source_data['title']} to {target_data['title']} (matching: {link})") print("Minimum click path length: 1") break if not direct_link: print(f"\nNo direct link from {source_data['title']} to {target_data['title']}") print("Need to explore indirect paths...") # Build a graph of the known Wikipedia links graph = nx.DiGraph() # Add nodes and edges for source page source_normalized = source_data['title'].lower().replace(' ', '_') graph.add_node(source_normalized) target_normalized = target_data['title'].lower().replace(' ', '_') graph.add_node(target_normalized) if 'links' in source_data: for link in source_data['links']: link_normalized = link.lower().replace(' ', '_') graph.add_node(link_normalized) graph.add_edge(source_normalized, link_normalized) # Add nodes and edges for target page if 'links' in target_data: for link in target_data['links']: link_normalized = link.lower().replace(' ', '_') graph.add_node(link_normalized) graph.add_edge(target_normalized, link_normalized) # Check for common links (two-click path) common_links = set() if 'links' in source_data and 'links' in target_data: source_links = {link.lower().replace(' ', '_') for link in source_data['links']} target_links = {link.lower().replace(' ', '_') for link in target_data['links']} common_links = source_links.intersection(target_links) if common_links: print(f"\nFound {len(common_links)} common links between source and target:") for i, link in enumerate(sorted(common_links)[:10]): # Show first 10 common links print(f" {i+1}. {link.replace('_', ' ')}") if len(common_links) > 10: print(f" ... and {len(common_links) - 10} more") print("\nMinimum click path length: 2") print(f"Path: {source_data['title']} -> [any common link] -> {target_data['title']}") else: print("\nNo common links found between source and target pages.") print("Need more data or a breadth-first search to find the shortest path.") print("This would require fetching additional Wikipedia pages.") # Try to find a path with the data we have try: if nx.has_path(graph, source_normalized, target_normalized): shortest_path = nx.shortest_path(graph, source_normalized, target_normalized) print(f"\nFound a path in our current graph: {shortest_path}") print(f"Minimum click path length: {len(shortest_path)-1}") else: reverse_path = nx.shortest_path(graph, target_normalized, source_normalized) if nx.has_path(graph, target_normalized, source_normalized) else None if reverse_path: print(f"\nFound a reverse path (target to source): {reverse_path}") print(f"Reverse path length: {len(reverse_path)-1}") else: print("\nCurrent graph does not have a complete path between source and target.") print("We would need to explore more pages to find the complete path.") except nx.NetworkXNoPath: print("\nNo path found in our current graph.") else: print("\nMissing link data for one or both pages.") print("Need to collect more data to determine the click path.") else: print("\nMissing data for one or both pages. Cannot analyze the click path.") print(f"Have source page data: {source_data is not None}") print(f"Have target page data: {target_data is not None}") # If we don't have the data, suggest what we need to do if not (source_data or target_data): print("\nWe need to fetch both Wikipedia pages to analyze the click path:") print(f"1. {source_page}") print(f"2. {target_page}") elif not source_data: print(f"\nWe need to fetch the source page: {source_page}") else: print(f"\nWe need to fetch the target page: {target_page}") print("\nCOMPLETE ANALYSIS SUMMARY:") print("=" * 50) if source_data and target_data: if direct_link: print(f"A direct link exists from '{source_page}' to '{target_page}'") print("Minimum click path length: 1") elif 'links' in source_data and 'links' in target_data and common_links: print(f"No direct link, but {len(common_links)} common links found") print("Minimum click path length: 2") print(f"Example path: {source_page} -> {list(common_links)[0].replace('_', ' ')} -> {target_page}") else: print("No direct link or common link found with current data") print("Would need to explore more pages to determine exact path length") else: print("Insufficient data to determine the minimum click path") print("Need to fetch Wikipedia page content for analysis")

import os import json # First, let's check the workspace directory workspace_dir = os.environ.get('WORKSPACE_DIR', 'workspace') print(f"Looking for navigation analysis files in: {workspace_dir}") # List files in the workspace files = [] if os.path.exists(workspace_dir): files = os.listdir(workspace_dir) print(f"Found {len(files)} files in the workspace:") for file in sorted(files): file_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, file) if os.path.isfile(file_path): size = os.path.getsize(file_path) print(f" - {file} ({size} bytes)") else: print(f"Error: Workspace directory '{workspace_dir}' not found.") # Look specifically for the navigation analysis JSON files navigation_files = [file for file in files if 'navigation' in file.lower() and file.endswith('.json')] print(f" Found {len(navigation_files)} navigation analysis files: {navigation_files}") # Define function to load and explore JSON files def explore_json(file_path): print(f"Exploring: {file_path}") try: with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: data = json.load(f) print(f"File type: {type(data)}") if isinstance(data, dict): print(f"Top-level keys: {list(data.keys())}") # Print key details for each top-level key for key, value in data.items(): print(f" [{key}]:") if isinstance(value, dict): print(f" Dictionary with {len(value)} keys: {list(value.keys())}") # Special handling for navigation_paths and summary if key == 'navigation_paths' and 'direct_links' in value: print(f" Direct links: {value['direct_links']}") if key == 'summary': for sk, sv in value.items(): print(f" {sk}: {sv}") elif isinstance(value, list): print(f" List with {len(value)} items") if value and len(value) > 0: print(f" First item: {value[0]}") else: print(f" {value}") return data else: print(f"Not a dictionary: {type(data)}") return data except Exception as e: print(f"Error reading file: {e}") return None # Load the primary navigation analysis file if available analysis_data = None detailed_data = None for file in navigation_files: file_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, file) print(f" {'='*60}") if 'detailed' in file: detailed_data = explore_json(file_path) elif file == 'wikipedia_navigation_analysis.json': analysis_data = explore_json(file_path) elif file == 'navigation_summary.json': summary_data = explore_json(file_path) print(f" {'='*60}") print("MINIMUM CLICK PATH ANALYSIS:") print(f"{'='*60}") # Analyze the data to find the minimum click path if analysis_data: print("Using data from wikipedia_navigation_analysis.json") # Extract key information source_page = "The Lord of the Rings" target_page = "A Song of Ice and Fire" # Check for direct links direct_links = analysis_data.get('navigation_paths', {}).get('direct_links', {}) source_to_target = direct_links.get(f"{source_page.replace(' ', '_')}_to_{target_page.replace(' ', '_')}", False) target_to_source = direct_links.get(f"{target_page.replace(' ', '_')}_to_{source_page.replace(' ', '_')}", False) summary = analysis_data.get('summary', {}) direct_path_exists = summary.get('direct_path_exists', False) direct_paths = summary.get('direct_paths', []) if source_to_target: print(f" âœ“ Direct link exists: {source_page} â†’ {target_page}") print("Minimum click path length: 1") elif target_to_source: print(f" âœ“ Direct link exists: {target_page} â†’ {source_page}") print(f"Note: This is in the reverse direction (from target to source)") print("Minimum click path length: 1 (in reverse direction)") else: print(f" âœ— No direct link from {source_page} to {target_page} or vice versa") # Check for common links (2-click path) common_links = analysis_data.get('navigation_paths', {}).get('common_links', []) if common_links: print(f" Common links between {source_page} and {target_page}:") for i, link in enumerate(common_links[:10]): print(f" {i+1}. {link}") if len(common_links) > 10: print(f" ... and {len(common_links) - 10} more") print(f" âœ“ Two-click path exists: {source_page} â†’ [common link] â†’ {target_page}") print("Minimum click path length: 2") else: print(f" âœ— No common links between {source_page} and {target_page}") # Check the summary for more details intermediate_paths_count = summary.get('intermediate_paths_count', 0) top_intermediate_pages = summary.get('top_intermediate_pages', []) if intermediate_paths_count > 0: print(f" Found {intermediate_paths_count} intermediate paths between the pages") if top_intermediate_pages: print("Top intermediate pages:") for i, page in enumerate(top_intermediate_pages[:5]): if isinstance(page, dict) and 'title' in page: print(f" {i+1}. {page['title']}") else: print(f" {i+1}. {page}") # Final conclusion on minimum click path print(f" {'='*60}") print("CONCLUSION:") if source_to_target: print(f"The minimum click path from {source_page} to {target_page} is 1 click.") print(f"Direct link: {source_page} â†’ {target_page}") elif target_to_source: print(f"There is a 1-click path in the reverse direction: {target_page} â†’ {source_page}") if common_links: print(f"In the forward direction, the minimum click path is 2 clicks.") print(f"Example path: {source_page} â†’ {common_links[0]} â†’ {target_page}") else: print(f"In the forward direction, more research is needed.") elif common_links: print(f"The minimum click path from {source_page} to {target_page} is 2 clicks.") print(f"Example path: {source_page} â†’ {common_links[0]} â†’ {target_page}") else: print(f"Based on the available data, the minimum click path length could not be determined.") print(f"The analysis found {intermediate_paths_count} intermediate paths, suggesting a path exists but requires more steps.") # Check if we have a visualization visualization_file = summary.get('visualization_file') if visualization_file: print(f" Visualization available at: {visualization_file}") elif detailed_data: print("Using data from the detailed analysis file") # Similar analysis as above, using detailed_data # This is a fallback if the main analysis file is not available summary = detailed_data.get('summary', {}) direct_path_exists = summary.get('direct_path_exists', False) if direct_path_exists: print(f"âœ“ Direct path exists between the pages") if 'direct_paths' in summary: print(f"Direct paths: {summary['direct_paths']}") else: print(f"âœ— No direct path found between the pages") intermediate_paths_count = summary.get('intermediate_paths_count', 0) top_intermediate_pages = summary.get('top_intermediate_pages', []) if intermediate_paths_count > 0: print(f"Found {intermediate_paths_count} intermediate paths between the pages") if top_intermediate_pages: print("Top intermediate pages:") for i, page in enumerate(top_intermediate_pages[:5]): if isinstance(page, dict) and 'title' in page: print(f" {i+1}. {page['title']}") else: print(f" {i+1}. {page}") # Conclusion for detailed data print(f" {'='*60}") print("CONCLUSION (from detailed analysis):") if direct_path_exists: print("The minimum click path is 1 click (direct link exists).") elif intermediate_paths_count > 0: print("The minimum click path appears to be 2 clicks (through an intermediate page).") else: print("Could not determine the minimum click path from the available data.") else: print("Could not find the required navigation analysis data.") print("Please check that the workspace contains the navigation analysis files.") print(f" {'='*60}")

import os import json # First, let's check the workspace directory workspace_dir = os.environ.get('WORKSPACE_DIR', 'workspace') print(f"Looking for navigation analysis files in: {workspace_dir}") # List files in the workspace files = [] if os.path.exists(workspace_dir): files = os.listdir(workspace_dir) print(f"Found {len(files)} files in the workspace:") for file in sorted(files): file_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, file) if os.path.isfile(file_path): size = os.path.getsize(file_path) print(f" - {file} ({size} bytes)") else: print(f"Error: Workspace directory '{workspace_dir}' not found.") # Look specifically for the navigation analysis JSON files navigation_files = [file for file in files if 'navigation' in file.lower() and file.endswith('.json')] print(f" Found {len(navigation_files)} navigation analysis files: {navigation_files}") # Define function to load and explore JSON files def explore_json(file_path): print(f"Exploring: {file_path}") try: with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: data = json.load(f) print(f"File type: {type(data)}") if isinstance(data, dict): print(f"Top-level keys: {list(data.keys())}") # Print key details for each top-level key for key, value in data.items(): print(f" [{key}]:") if isinstance(value, dict): print(f" Dictionary with {len(value)} keys: {list(value.keys())}") # Special handling for navigation_paths and summary if key == 'navigation_paths' and 'direct_links' in value: print(f" Direct links: {value['direct_links']}") if key == 'summary': for sk, sv in value.items(): print(f" {sk}: {sv}") elif isinstance(value, list): print(f" List with {len(value)} items") if value and len(value) > 0: print(f" First item: {value[0]}") else: print(f" {value}") return data else: print(f"Not a dictionary: {type(data)}") return data except Exception as e: print(f"Error reading file: {e}") return None # Load the primary navigation analysis file if available analysis_data = None detailed_data = None for file in navigation_files: file_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, file) print(f" {'='*60}") if 'detailed' in file: detailed_data = explore_json(file_path) elif file == 'wikipedia_navigation_analysis.json': analysis_data = explore_json(file_path) elif file == 'navigation_summary.json': summary_data = explore_json(file_path) print(f" {'='*60}") print("MINIMUM CLICK PATH ANALYSIS:") print(f"{'='*60}") # import os import json # First, let's check the workspace directory workspace_dir = os.environ.get('WORKSPACE_DIR', 'workspace') print(f"Looking for navigation analysis files in: {workspace_dir}") # List files in the workspace files = [] if os.path.exists(workspace_dir): files = os.listdir(workspace_dir) print(f"Found {len(files)} files in the workspace:") for file in sorted(files): file_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, file) if os.path.isfile(file_path): size = os.path.getsize(file_path) print(f" - {file} ({size} bytes)") else: print(f"Error: Workspace directory '{workspace_dir}' not found.") # Look specifically for the navigation analysis JSON files navigation_files = [file for file in files if 'navigation' in file.lower() and file.endswith('.json')] print("") print(f"Found {len(navigation_files)} navigation analysis files: {navigation_files}") # Define function to load and explore JSON files def explore_json(file_path): print(f"Exploring: {file_path}") try: with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: data = json.load(f) print(f"File type: {type(data)}") if isinstance(data, dict): print(f"Top-level keys: {list(data.keys())}") # Print key details for each top-level key for key, value in data.items(): print("") print(f"[{key}]:") if isinstance(value, dict): print(f" Dictionary with {len(value)} keys: {list(value.keys())}") # Special handling for navigation_paths and summary if key == 'navigation_paths' and 'direct_links' in value: print(f" Direct links: {value['direct_links']}") if key == 'summary': for sk, sv in value.items(): print(f" {sk}: {sv}") elif isinstance(value, list): print(f" List with {len(value)} items") if value and len(value) > 0: print(f" First item: {value[0]}") else: print(f" {value}") return data else: print(f"Not a dictionary: {type(data)}") return data except Exception as e: print(f"Error reading file: {e}") return None # Load the primary navigation analysis file if available analysis_data = None detailed_data = None summary_data = None for file in navigation_files: file_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, file) print("") print("="*60) if 'detailed' in file: detailed_data = explore_json(file_path) elif file == 'wikipedia_navigation_analysis.json': analysis_data = explore_json(file_path) elif file == 'navigation_summary.json': summary_data = explore_json(file_path) print("") print("="*60) print("MINIMUM CLICK PATH ANALYSIS:") print("="*60) # Analyze the data to find the minimum click path if analysis_data: print("Using data from wikipedia_navigation_analysis.json") # Extract key information source_page = "The Lord of the Rings" target_page = "A Song of Ice and Fire" # Check for direct links direct_links = analysis_data.get('navigation_paths', {}).get('direct_links', {}) source_to_target = direct_links.get(f"{source_page.replace(' ', '_')}_to_{target_page.replace(' ', '_')}", False) target_to_source = direct_links.get(f"{target_page.replace(' ', '_')}_to_{source_page.replace(' ', '_')}", False) summary = analysis_data.get('summary', {}) direct_path_exists = summary.get('direct_path_exists', False) direct_paths = summary.get('direct_paths', []) print("") if source_to_target: print(f"âœ“ Direct link exists: {source_page} â†’ {target_page}") print("Minimum click path length: 1") elif target_to_source: print(f"âœ“ Direct link exists: {target_page} â†’ {source_page}") print(f"Note: This is in the reverse direction (from target to source)") print("Minimum click path length: 1 (in reverse direction)") else: print(f"âœ— No direct link from {source_page} to {target_page} or vice versa") # Check for common links (2-click path) common_links = analysis_data.get('navigation_paths', {}).get('common_links', []) print("") if common_links: print(f"Common links between {source_page} and {target_page}:") for i, link in enumerate(common_links[:10]): print(f" {i+1}. {link}") if len(common_links) > 10: print(f" ... and {len(common_links) - 10} more") print("") print(f"âœ“ Two-click path exists: {source_page} â†’ [common link] â†’ {target_page}") print("Minimum click path length: 2") else: print(f"âœ— No common links between {source_page} and {target_page}") # Check the summary for more details intermediate_paths_count = summary.get('intermediate_paths_count', 0) top_intermediate_pages = summary.get('top_intermediate_pages', []) print("") if intermediate_paths_count > 0: print(f"Found {intermediate_paths_count} intermediate paths between the pages") if top_intermediate_pages: print("Top intermediate pages:") for i, page in enumerate(top_intermediate_pages[:5]): if isinstance(page, dict) and 'title' in page: print(f" {i+1}. {page['title']}") else: print(f" {i+1}. {page}") # Final conclusion on minimum click path print("") print("="*60) print("CONCLUSION:") if source_to_target: print(f"The minimum click path from {source_page} to {target_page} is 1 click.") print(f"Direct link: {source_page} â†’ {target_page}") elif target_to_source: print(f"There is a 1-click path in the reverse direction: {target_page} â†’ {source_page}") if common_links: print(f"In the forward direction, the minimum click path is 2 clicks.") print(f"Example path: {source_page} â†’ {common_links[0]} â†’ {target_page}") else: print(f"In the forward direction, more research is needed.") elif common_links: print(f"The minimum click path from {source_page} to {target_page} is 2 clicks.") print(f"Example path: {source_page} â†’ {common_links[0]} â†’ {target_page}") else: print(f"Based on the available data, the minimum click path length could not be determined.") print(f"The analysis found {intermediate_paths_count} intermediate paths, suggesting a path exists but requires more steps.") # Check if we have a visualization visualization_file = summary.get('visualization_file') if visualization_file: print("") print(f"Visualization available at: {visualization_file}") elif detailed_data: print("Using data from the detailed analysis file") # Similar analysis as above, using detailed_data # This is a fallback if the main analysis file is not available summary = detailed_data.get('summary', {}) direct_path_exists = summary.get('direct_path_exists', False) print("") if direct_path_exists: print(f"âœ“ Direct path exists between the pages") if 'direct_paths' in summary: print(f"Direct paths: {summary['direct_paths']}") else: print(f"âœ— No direct path found between the pages") intermediate_paths_count = summary.get('intermediate_paths_count', 0) top_intermediate_pages = summary.get('top_intermediate_pages', []) print("") if intermediate_paths_count > 0: print(f"Found {intermediate_paths_count} intermediate paths between the pages") if top_intermediate_pages: print("Top intermediate pages:") for i, page in enumerate(top_intermediate_pages[:5]): if isinstance(page, dict) and 'title' in page: print(f" {i+1}. {page['title']}") else: print(f" {i+1}. {page}") # Conclusion for detailed data print("") print("="*60) print("CONCLUSION (from detailed analysis):") if direct_path_exists: print("The minimum click path is 1 click (direct link exists).") elif intermediate_paths_count > 0: print("The minimum click path appears to be 2 clicks (through an intermediate page).") else: print("Could not determine the minimum click path from the available data.") else: print("Could not find the required navigation analysis data.") print("Please check that the workspace contains the navigation analysis files.") print("") print("="*60)

import os import json import pprint # Define workspace directory and print a header workspace_dir = os.environ.get('WORKSPACE_DIR', 'workspace') print(f"WIKIPEDIA CLICK PATH ANALYSIS: 'The Lord of the Rings' â†’ 'A Song of Ice and Fire'") print("="*80) # Step 1: Find and load the relevant navigation analysis files print("STEP 1: LOCATING NAVIGATION ANALYSIS FILES") print("-"*50) nav_files = [] if os.path.exists(workspace_dir): files = os.listdir(workspace_dir) # Print directory contents for reference print(f"Found {len(files)} files in workspace:") for file in sorted(files): file_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, file) if os.path.isfile(file_path): size = os.path.getsize(file_path) if 'navigation' in file.lower() and file.endswith('.json'): nav_files.append(file) print(f" * {file} ({size:,} bytes) [NAVIGATION DATA]") else: print(f" - {file} ({size:,} bytes)") else: print(f"Warning: Workspace directory '{workspace_dir}' not found") if not nav_files: print("\nNo navigation analysis files found. Cannot proceed with analysis.") exit() print(f"\nFound {len(nav_files)} navigation analysis files for examination.") # Step 2: Load and examine the primary navigation analysis file print("\nSTEP 2: EXAMINING NAVIGATION DATA STRUCTURE") print("-"*50) # Primary navigation file to use (prioritizing the most informative ones) primary_file = None for filename in ['wikipedia_navigation_analysis.json', 'wikipedia_navigation_analysis_detailed.json', 'navigation_summary.json']: if filename in nav_files: primary_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, filename) print(f"Selected primary navigation file: {filename}") break if not primary_file: primary_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, nav_files[0]) print(f"Using first available navigation file: {nav_files[0]}") # Load the navigation data print(f"Loading navigation data from: {primary_file}") try: with open(primary_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: nav_data = json.load(f) # Examine structure without diving too deep into content print("\nNavigation data structure:") if isinstance(nav_data, dict): print(f"Top-level keys: {', '.join(nav_data.keys())}") # Look for key sections that would contain path information for key in ['navigation_paths', 'summary', 'potential_paths']: if key in nav_data and isinstance(nav_data[key], dict): print(f"\n'{key}' section contains: {', '.join(nav_data[key].keys())}") else: print(f"Unexpected format: {type(nav_data)}") except Exception as e: print(f"Error loading navigation data: {e}") exit() # Step 3: Extract and analyze the path information print("\nSTEP 3: EXTRACTING PATH INFORMATION") print("-"*50) source_page = "The Lord of the Rings" target_page = "A Song of Ice and Fire" source_key = source_page.replace(" ", "_") target_key = target_page.replace(" ", "_") print(f"Analyzing path from '{source_page}' to '{target_page}'") # Check for direct links between pages direct_path_exists = False direct_path_direction = None direct_links = {} # First, check in navigation_paths.direct_links if 'navigation_paths' in nav_data and 'direct_links' in nav_data['navigation_paths']: direct_links = nav_data['navigation_paths']['direct_links'] source_to_target_key = f"{source_key}_to_{target_key}" target_to_source_key = f"{target_key}_to_{source_key}" if source_to_target_key in direct_links: print(f"\nDirect link check (sourceâ†’target): {direct_links[source_to_target_key]}") if direct_links[source_to_target_key]: direct_path_exists = True direct_path_direction = "forward" if target_to_source_key in direct_links: print(f"Direct link check (targetâ†’source): {direct_links[target_to_source_key]}") if direct_links[target_to_source_key]: direct_path_exists = True direct_path_direction = "reverse" # Second, check in summary.direct_path_exists if 'summary' in nav_data: summary = nav_data['summary'] if 'direct_path_exists' in summary: print(f"Summary indicates direct path exists: {summary['direct_path_exists']}") if summary['direct_path_exists'] and not direct_path_exists: print("Note: Summary indicates a direct path but direction is unclear") direct_path_exists = True # Check for listed direct paths if 'direct_paths' in summary and summary['direct_paths']: print(f"\nDirect paths listed in summary:") for path in summary['direct_paths']: print(f" - {path}") if source_page in path and target_page in path: if path.index(source_page) < path.index(target_page): direct_path_direction = "forward" else: direct_path_direction = "reverse" # Check intermediate paths from summary intermediate_paths_count = 0 intermediate_pages = [] if 'summary' in nav_data: summary = nav_data['summary'] if 'intermediate_paths_count' in summary: intermediate_paths_count = summary['intermediate_paths_count'] print(f"\nIntermediate paths count from summary: {intermediate_paths_count}") if 'top_intermediate_pages' in summary and summary['top_intermediate_pages']: intermediate_pages = summary['top_intermediate_pages'] if intermediate_pages: print("Top intermediate pages from summary:") for i, page in enumerate(intermediate_pages[:5]): if isinstance(page, dict) and 'title' in page: title = page['title'].replace('_', ' ') print(f" {i+1}. {title}") else: print(f" {i+1}. {page}") # Construct example path if common_links and isinstance(common_links[0], dict) and 'title' in common_links[0]: intermediate = common_links[0]['title'].replace('_', ' ') elif intermediate_pages and isinstance(intermediate_pages[0], dict) and 'title' in intermediate_pages[0]: intermediate = intermediate_pages[0]['title'].replace('_', ' ') elif common_links: intermediate = str(common_links[0]).replace('_', ' ') elif intermediate_pages: intermediate = str(intermediate_pages[0]).replace('_', ' ') else: intermediate = "[intermediate page]" path_example = f"{source_page} â†’ {intermediate} â†’ {target_page}" print(f"Example path: {path_example}") else: print("âœ— No clear path found between pages") print("Analysis could not determine minimum click path") #
