import os import json def print_json_structure(data, indent=0, max_level=2, current_level=0): """Helper function to print the structure of JSON data without showing all content""" if current_level >= max_level: print(' ' * indent + '...') return if isinstance(data, dict): print(' ' * indent + '{') for key, value in data.items(): print(' ' * (indent + 2) + f'"{key}": ', end='') print_json_structure(value, indent + 2, max_level, current_level + 1) print(' ' * indent + '}') elif isinstance(data, list): if len(data) == 0: print('[]') else: print(f'[{len(data)} items]') if current_level < max_level - 1 and len(data) > 0: print(' ' * (indent + 2), end='') print_json_structure(data[0], indent + 2, max_level, current_level + 1) if len(data) > 1: print(' ' * (indent + 2) + '...') else: print(repr(str(data)[:50]) + ('...' if len(str(data)) > 50 else '')) # First, let's check for the navigation analysis files in the workspace print("Looking for Wikipedia navigation data in workspace...") navigation_files = [ 'workspace/wikipedia_navigation_analysis.json', 'workspace/wikipedia_navigation_analysis_detailed.json' ] # Store our findings about the navigation path path_info = { 'source': 'The Lord of the Rings', 'target': 'A Song of Ice and Fire', 'path_found': False } # Examine each navigation analysis file for file_path in navigation_files: if os.path.exists(file_path): print(f"\nFound navigation file: {file_path}") try: with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: data = json.load(f) # Print top-level structure to understand the file format print("\nTop-level structure:") print(list(data.keys())) # Check if navigation_paths exists and what structure it has if 'navigation_paths' in data: nav_paths = data['navigation_paths'] print("\nNavigation paths structure:") print(list(nav_paths.keys())) # Check for direct link (1-click path) if 'direct_links' in nav_paths: direct_links = nav_paths['direct_links'] print("\nDirect links information:") print(direct_links) # Check for direct link from Lord of the Rings to Song of Ice and Fire direct_path_key = 'The_Lord_of_the_Rings_to_A_Song_of_Ice_and_Fire' if direct_path_key in direct_links: direct_path_exists = direct_links[direct_path_key] if direct_path_exists: print("\nâœ“ DIRECT PATH FOUND (1 click)") path_info['path_found'] = True path_info['clicks'] = 1 path_info['path'] = [path_info['source'], path_info['target']] path_info['via'] = 'Direct link' break else: print("\nâœ— No direct path between the pages") # If no direct path, check for common links (2-click path) if not path_info['path_found'] and 'common_links' in nav_paths: common_links = nav_paths['common_links'] print("\nCommon links structure:") print(f"Type: {type(common_links)}, Length: {len(common_links)}") if isinstance(common_links, list) and len(common_links) > 0: # Print first item to understand structure print("First common link item:") print(common_links[0]) # Extract the first (most relevant) intermediate page if 'text' in common_links[0]: intermediate_page = common_links[0]['text'] print(f"\nâœ“ FOUND 2-CLICK PATH via '{intermediate_page}'") path_info['path_found'] = True path_info['clicks'] = 2 path_info['path'] = [path_info['source'], intermediate_page, path_info['target']] path_info['via'] = f"Intermediate page: {intermediate_page}" # Also store the top 5 alternative intermediate pages path_info['alternative_intermediates'] = [] for i, link in enumerate(common_links[1:6]): if 'text' in link: category = link.get('category', 'Unknown') path_info['alternative_intermediates'].append({ 'page': link['text'], 'category': category }) break # If we still don't have a path, check summary information if not path_info['path_found'] and 'summary' in data: summary = data['summary'] print("\nSummary information:") print(list(summary.keys())) if 'top_intermediate_pages' in summary and summary['top_intermediate_pages']: intermediate_pages = summary['top_intermediate_pages'] if isinstance(intermediate_pages, list) and len(intermediate_pages) > 0: # Get the first/best intermediate page first_page = intermediate_pages[0] if isinstance(first_page, dict) and 'text' in first_page: intermediate = first_page['text'] print(f"\nâœ“ FOUND 2-CLICK PATH (from summary) via '{intermediate}'") path_info['path_found'] = True path_info['clicks'] = 2 path_info['path'] = [path_info['source'], intermediate, path_info['target']] path_info['via'] = f"Intermediate page from summary: {intermediate}" break except Exception as e: print(f"Error processing {file_path}: {e}") # Create a complete result with our findings print("\n" + "="*60) print("WIKIPEDIA SHORTEST PATH RESULTS") print("="*60) if path_info['path_found']: result = { "source": path_info['source'], "target": path_info['target'], "clicks": path_info['clicks'], "path": path_info['path'], "path_description": f"The shortest path from '{path_info['source']}' to '{path_info['target']}' " f"requires {path_info['clicks']} clicks" } if path_info['clicks'] == 2: intermediate = path_info['path'][1] result["path_description"] += f" through the intermediate page '{intermediate}'." # Add alternative intermediate pages if we have them if 'alternative_intermediates' in path_info: result["alternative_intermediates"] = path_info['alternative_intermediates'] else: result["path_description"] += "." # Save the result to a file with open('workspace/shortest_wiki_path_result.json', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(result, f, indent=2) print(f"Result saved to workspace/shortest_wiki_path_result.json") # Display the results print(f"\nSource: {result['source']}") print(f"Target: {result['target']}") print(f"Minimum clicks required: {result['clicks']}") print(f"Path: {' â†’ '.join(result['path'])}") print(f"\nDescription: {result['path_description']}") # If we have alternative paths, show them if 'alternative_intermediates' in result and result['alternative_intermediates']: print("\nAlternative intermediate pages:") for i, alt in enumerate(result['alternative_intermediates']): print(f" {i+1}. {alt['page']} (Category: {alt['category']})") # Create a comprehensive markdown summary with open('workspace/wikipedia_navigation_summary.md', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as md_file: md_file.write(f"# Shortest Path Between Wikipedia Pages\n\n") md_file.write(f"## Overview\n\n") md_file.write(f"This analysis determines the shortest clickable path between two Wikipedia pages ") md_file.write(f"based on their July 3, 2023 versions.\n\n") md_file.write(f"## Path Details\n\n") md_file.write(f"- **Source Page:** {result['source']}\n") md_file.write(f"- **Target Page:** {result['target']}\n") md_file.write(f"- **Minimum Clicks Required:** {result['clicks']}\n") md_file.write(f"- **Complete Path:** `{' â†’ '.join(result['path'])}`\n\n") if result['clicks'] == 2: md_file.write(f"## Intermediate Page\n\n") md_file.write(f"To navigate from '{result['source']}' to '{result['target']}', ") md_file.write(f"a user must click through the intermediate page **{result['path'][1]}**.\n\n") if 'alternative_intermediates' in result and result['alternative_intermediates']: md_file.write(f"### Alternative Intermediate Pages\n\n") md_file.write(f"While '{result['path'][1]}' provides the most direct path, ") md_file.write(f"the following pages could also serve as intermediate steps:\n\n") for alt in result['alternative_intermediates']: md_file.write(f"- **{alt['page']}** (Category: {alt['category']})\n") md_file.write(f"\n## Conclusion\n\n") md_file.write(f"{result['path_description']}") print(f"\nComprehensive summary saved to workspace/wikipedia_navigation_summary.md") else: print("Could not find a path between the Wikipedia pages from the available data.") print("Consider checking the HTML files directly for links or using a different approach.")

Python Code python
import os import json import pprint print("Finding the shortest path between Wikipedia pages...") # Define paths to JSON files that contain our navigation analysis navigation_files = [ 'workspace/wikipedia_navigation_analysis.json', 'workspace/wikipedia_navigation_analysis_detailed.json' ] # Source and target page definitions source_page = "The Lord of the Rings" target_page = "A Song of Ice and Fire" print(f"Analyzing navigation path from '{source_page}' to '{target_page}'") print(f"Based on Wikipedia versions from July 3, 2023") # Function to inspect and analyze navigation files def analyze_navigation_data(): path_info = None for file_path in navigation_files: if not os.path.exists(file_path): print(f"File not found: {file_path}") continue print(f"\nExamining file: {file_path}") try: with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: data = json.load(f) print("Successfully loaded JSON data") # Check for direct links first (would be a 1-click path) if 'navigation_paths' in data and 'direct_links' in data['navigation_paths']: direct_links = data['navigation_paths']['direct_links'] print("\nDirect links information:") print(direct_links) # Check if there's a direct path from source to target direct_path_key = f"{source_page.replace(' ', '_')}_to_{target_page.replace(' ', '_')}" if direct_path_key in direct_links: direct_path_exists = direct_links[direct_path_key] if direct_path_exists: print(f"\nâœ“ DIRECT PATH EXISTS: {source_page} â†’ {target_page}") return { 'clicks': 1, 'path': [source_page, target_page], 'path_type': 'direct', 'description': f"Direct path from '{source_page}' to '{target_page}' requires just 1 click." } else: print(f"\nâœ— No direct path from {source_page} to {target_page}") # If no direct path, look for intermediate pages (2-click paths) if 'navigation_paths' in data and 'common_links' in data['navigation_paths']: common_links = data['navigation_paths']['common_links'] # Verify common_links is a list and has items if isinstance(common_links, list) and common_links: print(f"\nFound {len(common_links)} potential intermediate pages") # Get the best intermediate page (first in the list) best_intermediate = common_links[0]['text'] print(f"Best intermediate page: {best_intermediate}") # Get additional intermediates for completeness alternative_pages = [] for i, link in enumerate(common_links[1:6]): # Get next 5 alternatives page_info = { 'page': link['text'], 'category': link.get('category', 'Unknown') } alternative_pages.append(page_info) # Return the 2-click path info return { 'clicks': 2, 'path': [source_page, best_intermediate, target_page], 'path_type': 'intermediate', 'intermediate_page': best_intermediate, 'alternative_pages': alternative_pages, 'description': f"The shortest path from '{source_page}' to '{target_page}' requires 2 clicks through the intermediate page '{best_intermediate}'." } # If still no path, check summary section for top intermediate pages if 'summary' in data and 'top_intermediate_pages' in data['summary']: top_pages = data['summary']['top_intermediate_pages'] if isinstance(top_pages, list) and top_pages: # Extract the text from the first intermediate page if isinstance(top_pages[0], dict) and 'text' in top_pages[0]: best_intermediate = top_pages[0]['text'] print(f"\nBest intermediate page from summary: {best_intermediate}") # Return the 2-click path info return { 'clicks': 2, 'path': [source_page, best_intermediate, target_page], 'path_type': 'intermediate_from_summary', 'intermediate_page': best_intermediate, 'description': f"The shortest path from '{source_page}' to '{target_page}' requires 2 clicks through the intermediate page '{best_intermediate}'." } except Exception as e: print(f"Error processing {file_path}: {e}") return None # Main execution print("\n" + "="*60) print("FINDING SHORTEST WIKIPEDIA NAVIGATION PATH") print("="*60) path_info = analyze_navigation_data() if path_info: # Create the final result structure result = { "source": source_page, "target": target_page, "clicks": path_info['clicks'], "path": path_info['path'], "path_description": path_info['description'] } # Add alternative pages if available if 'alternative_pages' in path_info: result["alternative_intermediates"] = path_info['alternative_pages'] # Save the result to a JSON file with open('workspace/shortest_wiki_path_result.json', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(result, f, indent=2) print("\n" + "="*60) print("SHORTEST PATH RESULTS") print("="*60) print(f"Source: {result['source']}") print(f"Target: {result['target']}") print(f"Clicks required: {result['clicks']}") print(f"Path: {' â†’ '.join(result['path'])}") print(f"\nDescription: {result['path_description']}") # Show alternative pages if available if 'alternative_intermediates' in result: print("\nAlternative intermediate pages:") for i, alt in enumerate(result['alternative_intermediates']): print(f" {i+1}. {alt['page']} (Category: {alt['category']})") print(f"\nResult saved to workspace/shortest_wiki_path_result.json") # Create a markdown summary for better readability with open('workspace/navigation_path_summary.md', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as md: md.write(f"# Wikipedia Navigation Path Analysis\n\n") md.write(f"## Overview\n\n") md.write(f"This analysis determined the shortest clickable path between two Wikipedia pages based on their July 3, 2023 versions.\n\n") md.write(f"## Navigation Details\n\n") md.write(f"- **Source Page:** {result['source']}\n") md.write(f"- **Target Page:** {result['target']}\n") md.write(f"- **Minimum Clicks Required:** {result['clicks']}\n") md.write(f"- **Complete Path:** `{' â†’ '.join(result['path'])}`\n\n") if result['clicks'] == 2: md.write(f"## Intermediate Page\n\n") md.write(f"The navigation requires going through the **{result['path'][1]}** page.\n\n") if 'alternative_intermediates' in result: md.write(f"### Alternative Intermediate Pages\n\n") md.write(f"Other possible intermediate pages include:\n\n") for alt in result['alternative_intermediates']: md.write(f"- **{alt['page']}** (Category: {alt['category']})\n") md.write(f"\n## Conclusion\n\n") md.write(f"{result['path_description']}\n") print(f"Detailed summary saved to workspace/navigation_path_summary.md") else: print("\nCould not determine a path between the Wikipedia pages from the available data.")

Python Code python
import os import json # Function to create a markdown report with the shortest path information def create_path_report(path_info): with open('workspace/shortest_path_report.md', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as md_file: md_file.write(f"# Wikipedia Shortest Path Analysis\n\n") md_file.write(f"## Navigation Details\n\n") md_file.write(f"This analysis examines the shortest clickable path between two Wikipedia pages as they appeared on July 3, 2023.\n\n") md_file.write(f"- **Source Page:** {path_info['source']}\n") md_file.write(f"- **Target Page:** {path_info['target']}\n") md_file.write(f"- **Minimum Clicks Required:** {path_info['clicks']}\n") md_file.write(f"- **Complete Path:** `{' â†’ '.join(path_info['path'])}`\n\n") if len(path_info['path']) > 2: md_file.write(f"## Intermediate Page\n\n") md_file.write(f"To navigate from '{path_info['source']}' to '{path_info['target']}', ") md_file.write(f"the user must click through the intermediate page **{path_info['path'][1]}**.\n\n") if 'alternative_intermediates' in path_info: md_file.write(f"### Alternative Intermediate Pages\n\n") md_file.write(f"While '{path_info['path'][1]}' provides the optimal path, ") md_file.write(f"the following pages could also serve as intermediate steps:\n\n") for i, alt in enumerate(path_info['alternative_intermediates']): md_file.write(f"{i+1}. **{alt['page']}** (Category: {alt['category']})\n") md_file.write(f"\n## Conclusion\n\n") md_file.write(f"{path_info['path_description']}\n") # Start of main analysis print("Performing final analysis of Wikipedia navigation paths...") # Define the files we need to examine navigation_files = [ 'workspace/wikipedia_navigation_analysis.json', 'workspace/wikipedia_navigation_analysis_detailed.json', 'workspace/shortest_wiki_path_result.json' # Check if we already have results ] # Define source and target pages source_page = "The Lord of the Rings" target_page = "A Song of Ice and Fire" print(f"Analyzing shortest path: {source_page} â†’ {target_page}") # First check if we already have a results file results_file = 'workspace/shortest_wiki_path_result.json' if os.path.exists(results_file): print(f"Found existing results file: {results_file}") with open(results_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: result = json.load(f) print(f"\nLoaded existing path analysis results:") print(f"Source: {result['source']}") print(f"Target: {result['target']}") print(f"Clicks required: {result['clicks']}") print(f"Path: {' â†’ '.join(result['path'])}") # Create the final report create_path_report(result) print(f"\nFinal report created at workspace/shortest_path_report.md") # Print the final conclusion print("\n" + "="*70) print("FINAL CONCLUSION") print("="*70) print(f"The shortest path from '{source_page}' to '{target_page}' requires {result['clicks']} clicks:") print(f"Path: {' â†’ '.join(result['path'])}") if 'alternative_intermediates' in result and result['alternative_intermediates']: print("\nAlternative intermediate pages include:") for i, alt in enumerate(result['alternative_intermediates'][:3]): # Show top 3 print(f" {i+1}. {alt['page']} (Category: {alt['category']})") print("\nAnalysis complete.") else: # We need to analyze the navigation data from scratch print(f"No existing results found. Analyzing navigation data from source files...") # Check which navigation analysis files exist available_files = [f for f in navigation_files if os.path.exists(f)] if not available_files: print("Error: No navigation analysis files found in workspace!") else: print(f"Found {len(available_files)} navigation analysis files") # Process each file to find navigation path information path_info = None for file_path in available_files: if file_path.endswith('_result.json'): # Skip any result files continue print(f"\nExamining file: {file_path}") try: with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: data = json.load(f) # Check if file has navigation_paths structure if 'navigation_paths' in data: nav_paths = data['navigation_paths'] # First check for direct links (1-click path) if 'direct_links' in nav_paths: direct_links = nav_paths['direct_links'] direct_key = f"The_Lord_of_the_Rings_to_A_Song_of_Ice_and_Fire" if direct_key in direct_links: has_direct_path = direct_links[direct_key] print(f"Direct path exists: {has_direct_path}") if has_direct_path: path_info = { 'source': source_page, 'target': target_page, 'clicks': 1, 'path': [source_page, target_page], 'path_description': f"The shortest path from '{source_page}' to '{target_page}' requires just 1 click (direct link)." } break # Found direct path, no need to continue # If no direct path, look for common links (2-click paths) if not path_info and 'common_links' in nav_paths: common_links = nav_paths['common_links'] if isinstance(common_links, list) and common_links: # Get the primary intermediate page (first in list) best_intermediate = common_links[0]['text'] print(f"Best intermediate page: {best_intermediate}") # Also collect alternative intermediate pages alternatives = [] for i, link in enumerate(common_links[1:6]): # Get next 5 alternatives if 'text' in link: alternatives.append({ 'page': link['text'], 'category': link.get('category', 'Unknown') }) path_info = { 'source': source_page, 'target': target_page, 'clicks': 2, 'path': [source_page, best_intermediate, target_page], 'alternative_intermediates': alternatives, 'path_description': f"The shortest path from '{source_page}' to '{target_page}' requires 2 clicks through the intermediate page '{best_intermediate}'." } break # Found 2-click path with best intermediate page except Exception as e: print(f"Error processing {file_path}: {e}") # If we found a path, save the results if path_info: # Save to JSON file with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(path_info, f, indent=2) print(f"\nResults saved to {results_file}") # Create the final report create_path_report(path_info) print(f"Final report created at workspace/shortest_path_report.md") # Print the final conclusion print("\n" + "="*70) print("FINAL CONCLUSION") print("="*70) print(f"The shortest path from '{source_page}' to '{target_page}' requires {path_info['clicks']} clicks:") print(f"Path: {' â†’ '.join(path_info['path'])}") if 'alternative_intermediates' in path_info: print("\nAlternative intermediate pages include:") for i, alt in enumerate(path_info['alternative_intermediates'][:3]): # Show top 3 print(f" {i+1}. {alt['page']} (Category: {alt['category']})") print("\nAnalysis complete.") else: print("\nCould not determine shortest path from the available data.")
